After going over some of my needs, questions and concerns with Randy, I took the leap. Took it out today and put 200 rounds of Remington Range through it. Shot like a champ. No jams, no issues. Only thing that needs a little work is my shooting. Other than that, for the price point, it worked great for me.</div> <div class="Row"> By <span class="Text"> Jason</span> from <span class="Text"> Clinton</span></div> </div> </div> </td> </tr><tr> <td class="ReviewItem"> <div class="ItemStyle"> <div class="Title"> <span class="Subject"> Satisfied customer</span>, October 30, 2014</div> <div class="Content"> <div class="StarRating"> <img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/ShadeStar.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"></div> <div class="Row"> I purchased the Hi-Point .45 ACP here at Impact Guns. I wanted a fun to shoot range toy and personal defense weapon more accurate than a pistol. This is a good weapon for the price paid. It is made well and is accurate. I have put about 300 rounds down range and only had one failure to feed. Every round fed has fired. I am getting excellent groupings at my targets at 25 to 40 yards. I replaced the cheap rear iron sight with a quality holographic red dot sight. If you do place a red dot sight on this weapon, be advised it will most likely have to be adjusted to its lowest vertical setting due to the front sight post's odd/high placement. Bottom line: Its a reliable, fun weapon to shoot. It's also accurate. I'm glad I purchased it.</div> <div class="Row"> By <span class="Text"> Allen Venegas</span> from <span class="Text"> Washington State</span></div> </div> </div> </td> </tr> </tbody></table> </div> <div class="Paging"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_topNavigation"> <a id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_TopPrevLink" disabled="disabled">« Previous</a> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_lblPagingInfo"> | PAGE1 of 1 | </span> <a id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_TopNextLink" disabled="disabled">Next »</a> </div> </div> <div class="Spacer"> &nbsp;</div> <div> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_lblErrorMsg"></span></div> <div class="Spacer"> &nbsp;</div> </div> </div> </div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlAdditionalInformation" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="ShippingInfo"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlAdditionalInformation_ProductAdditionalInformation">This firearm ships to your local gun dealer/gun store (FFL dealer).
